class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Stream the video being downloaded to stdout\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -o - BaW_jenozKc\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch1 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eFORMAT SELECTION\u003c/h1\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-format-selection\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: FORMAT SELECTION\" href=\"#format-selection\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBy default, yt-dlp tries to download the best available quality if you \u003cstrong\u003edon't\u003c/strong\u003e pass any options.\nThis is generally equivalent to using \u003ccode\u003e-f bestvideo*+bestaudio/best\u003c/code\u003e. However, if multiple audiostreams is enabled (\u003ccode\u003e--audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e), the default format changes to \u003ccode\u003e-f bestvideo+bestaudio/best\u003c/code\u003e. Similarly, if ffmpeg is unavailable, or if you use yt-dlp to stream to \u003ccode\u003estdout\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e-o -\u003c/code\u003e), the default becomes \u003ccode\u003e-f best/bestvideo+bestaudio\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDeprecation warning\u003c/strong\u003e: Latest versions of yt-dlp can stream multiple formats to the stdout simultaneously using ffmpeg. So, in future versions, the default for this will be set to \u003ccode\u003e-f bv*+ba/b\u003c/code\u003e similar to normal downloads. If you want to preserve the \u003ccode\u003e-f b/bv+ba\u003c/code\u003e setting, it is recommended to explicitly specify it in the configuration options.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe general syntax for format selection is \u003ccode\u003e-f FORMAT\u003c/code\u003e (or \u003ccode\u003e--format FORMAT\u003c/code\u003e) where \u003ccode\u003eFORMAT\u003c/code\u003e is a \u003cem\u003eselector expression\u003c/em\u003e, i.e. an expression that describes format or formats you would like to download.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003etl;dr:\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ca href=\"#format-selection-examples\"\u003enavigate me to examples\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe simplest case is requesting a specific format; e.g. with \u003ccode\u003e-f 22\u003c/code\u003e you can download the format with format code equal to 22. You can get the list of available format codes for particular video using \u003ccode\u003e--list-formats\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e-F\u003c/code\u003e. Note that these format codes are extractor specific.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can also use a file extension (currently \u003ccode\u003e3gp\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eflv\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003em4a\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emp4\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eogg\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ewav\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e are supported) to download the best quality format of a particular file extension served as a single file, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f webm\u003c/code\u003e will download the best quality format with the \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e extension served as a single file.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can use \u003ccode\u003e-f -\u003c/code\u003e to interactively provide the format selector \u003cem\u003efor each video\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can also use special names to select particular edge case formats:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eall\u003c/code\u003e: Select \u003cstrong\u003eall formats\u003c/strong\u003e separately\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emergeall\u003c/code\u003e: Select and \u003cstrong\u003emerge all formats\u003c/strong\u003e (Must be used with \u003ccode\u003e--audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--video-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e or both)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eb*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebest*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality format that \u003cstrong\u003econtains either\u003c/strong\u003e a video or an audio or both (i.e.; \u003ccode\u003evcodec!=none or acodec!=none\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eb\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality format that \u003cstrong\u003econtains both\u003c/strong\u003e video and audio. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003ebest*[vcodec!=none][acodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebv\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebestvideo\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality \u003cstrong\u003evideo-only\u003c/strong\u003e format. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003ebest*[acodec=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebv*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebestvideo*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality format that \u003cstrong\u003econtains video\u003c/strong\u003e. It may also contain audio. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003ebest*[vcodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eba\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebestaudio\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality \u003cstrong\u003eaudio-only\u003c/strong\u003e format. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003ebest*[vcodec=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eba*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebestaudio*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the best quality format that \u003cstrong\u003econtains audio\u003c/strong\u003e. It may also contain video. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003ebest*[acodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/979#issuecomment-919629354\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/979/hovercard\"\u003eDo not use!\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ew*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworst*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality format that contains either a video or an audio\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ew\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworst\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality format that contains both video and audio. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003eworst*[vcodec!=none][acodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewv\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworstvideo\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality video-only format. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003eworst*[acodec=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewv*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworstvideo*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality format that contains video. It may also contain audio. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003eworst*[vcodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewa\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworstaudio\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality audio-only format. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003eworst*[vcodec=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewa*\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eworstaudio*\u003c/code\u003e: Select the worst quality format that contains audio. It may also contain video. Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003eworst*[acodec!=none]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor example, to download the worst quality video-only format you can use \u003ccode\u003e-f worstvideo\u003c/code\u003e. It is, however, recommended not to use \u003ccode\u003eworst\u003c/code\u003e and related options. When your format selector is \u003ccode\u003eworst\u003c/code\u003e, the format which is worst in all respects is selected. Most of the time, what you actually want is the video with the smallest filesize instead. So it is generally better to use \u003ccode\u003e-S +size\u003c/code\u003e or more rigorously, \u003ccode\u003e-S +size,+br,+res,+fps\u003c/code\u003e instead of \u003ccode\u003e-f worst\u003c/code\u003e. See \u003ca href=\"#sorting-formats\"\u003eSorting Formats\u003c/a\u003e for more details.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can select the n'th best format of a type by using \u003ccode\u003ebest\u0026lt;type\u0026gt;.\u0026lt;n\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e. For example, \u003ccode\u003ebest.2\u003c/code\u003e will select the 2nd best combined format. Similarly, \u003ccode\u003ebv*.3\u003c/code\u003e will select the 3rd best format that contains a video stream.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you want to download multiple videos, and they don't have the same formats available, you can specify the order of preference using slashes. Note that formats on the left hand side are preferred; e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f 22/17/18\u003c/code\u003e will download format 22 if it's available, otherwise it will download format 17 if it's available, otherwise it will download format 18 if it's available, otherwise it will complain that no suitable formats are available for download.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you want to download several formats of the same video use a comma as a separator, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f 22,17,18\u003c/code\u003e will download all these three formats, of course if they are available. Or a more sophisticated example combined with the precedence feature: \u003ccode\u003e-f 136/137/mp4/bestvideo,140/m4a/bestaudio\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can merge the video and audio of multiple formats into a single file using \u003ccode\u003e-f \u0026lt;format1\u0026gt;+\u0026lt;format2\u0026gt;+...\u003c/code\u003e (requires ffmpeg installed); e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f bestvideo+bestaudio\u003c/code\u003e will download the best video-only format, the best audio-only format and mux them together with ffmpeg.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDeprecation warning\u003c/strong\u003e: Since the \u003cem\u003ebelow\u003c/em\u003e described behavior is complex and counter-intuitive, this will be removed and multistreams will be enabled by default in the future. A new operator will be instead added to limit formats to single audio/video\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUnless \u003ccode\u003e--video-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e is used, all formats with a video stream except the first one are ignored. Similarly, unless \u003ccode\u003e--audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e is used, all formats with an audio stream except the first one are ignored. E.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f bestvideo+best+bestaudio --video-multistreams --audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e will download and merge all 3 given formats. The resulting file will have 2 video streams and 2 audio streams. But \u003ccode\u003e-f bestvideo+best+bestaudio --no-video-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e will download and merge only \u003ccode\u003ebestvideo\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ebestaudio\u003c/code\u003e. \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e is ignored since another format containing a video stream (\u003ccode\u003ebestvideo\u003c/code\u003e) has already been selected. The order of the formats is therefore important. \u003ccode\u003e-f best+bestaudio --no-audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e will download only \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e while \u003ccode\u003e-f bestaudio+best --no-audio-multistreams\u003c/code\u003e will ignore \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e and download only \u003ccode\u003ebestaudio\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eFiltering Formats\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-filtering-formats\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Filtering Formats\" href=\"#filtering-formats\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can also filter the video formats by putting a condition in brackets, as in \u003ccode\u003e-f \"best[height=720]\"\u003c/code\u003e (or \u003ccode\u003e-f \"[filesize\u0026gt;10M]\"\u003c/code\u003e since filters without a selector are interpreted as \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe following numeric meta fields can be used with comparisons \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;=\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e\u0026gt;=\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e=\u003c/code\u003e (equals), \u003ccode\u003e!=\u003c/code\u003e (not equals):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efilesize\u003c/code\u003e: The number of bytes, if known in advance\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efilesize_approx\u003c/code\u003e: An estimate for the number of bytes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewidth\u003c/code\u003e: Width of the video, if known\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eheight\u003c/code\u003e: Height of the video, if known\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003easpect_ratio\u003c/code\u003e: Aspect ratio of the video, if known\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etbr\u003c/code\u003e: Average bitrate of audio and video in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eabr\u003c/code\u003e: Average audio bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evbr\u003c/code\u003e: Average video bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003easr\u003c/code\u003e: Audio sampling rate in Hertz\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efps\u003c/code\u003e: Frame rate\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaudio_channels\u003c/code\u003e: The number of audio channels\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estretched_ratio\u003c/code\u003e: \u003ccode\u003ewidth:height\u003c/code\u003e of the video's pixels, if not square\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAlso filtering work for comparisons \u003ccode\u003e=\u003c/code\u003e (equals), \u003ccode\u003e^=\u003c/code\u003e (starts with), \u003ccode\u003e$=\u003c/code\u003e (ends with), \u003ccode\u003e*=\u003c/code\u003e (contains), \u003ccode\u003e~=\u003c/code\u003e (matches regex) and following string meta fields:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eurl\u003c/code\u003e: Video URL\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eext\u003c/code\u003e: File extension\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eacodec\u003c/code\u003e: Name of the audio codec in use\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evcodec\u003c/code\u003e: Name of the video codec in use\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econtainer\u003c/code\u003e: Name of the container format\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eprotocol\u003c/code\u003e: The protocol that will be used for the actual download, lower-case (\u003ccode\u003ehttp\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ehttps\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ertsp\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ertmp\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ertmpe\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emms\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ef4m\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eism\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ehttp_dash_segments\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003em3u8\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode\u003em3u8_native\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003elanguage\u003c/code\u003e: Language code\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edynamic_range\u003c/code\u003e: The dynamic range of the video\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat_id\u003c/code\u003e: A short description of the format\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat\u003c/code\u003e: A human-readable description of the format\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformat_note\u003c/code\u003e: Additional info about the format\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eresolution\u003c/code\u003e: Textual description of width and height\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAny string comparison may be prefixed with negation \u003ccode\u003e!\u003c/code\u003e in order to produce an opposite comparison, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e!*=\u003c/code\u003e (does not contain). The comparand of a string comparison needs to be quoted with either double or single quotes if it contains spaces or special characters other than \u003ccode\u003e._-\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote\u003c/strong\u003e: None of the aforementioned meta fields are guaranteed to be present since this solely depends on the metadata obtained by the particular extractor, i.e. the metadata offered by the website. Any other field made available by the extractor can also be used for filtering.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFormats for which the value is not known are excluded unless you put a question mark (\u003ccode\u003e?\u003c/code\u003e) after the operator. You can combine format filters, so \u003ccode\u003e-f \"bv[height\u0026lt;=?720][tbr\u0026gt;500]\"\u003c/code\u003e selects up to 720p videos (or videos where the height is not known) with a bitrate of at least 500 kbps. You can also use the filters with \u003ccode\u003eall\u003c/code\u003e to download all formats that satisfy the filter, e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f \"all[vcodec=none]\"\u003c/code\u003e selects all audio-only formats.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFormat selectors can also be grouped using parentheses; e.g. \u003ccode\u003e-f \"(mp4,webm)[height\u0026lt;480]\"\u003c/code\u003e will download the best pre-merged mp4 and webm formats with a height lower than 480.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSorting Formats\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-sorting-formats\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Sorting Formats\" href=\"#sorting-formats\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can change the criteria for being considered the \u003ccode\u003ebest\u003c/code\u003e by using \u003ccode\u003e-S\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e--format-sort\u003c/code\u003e). The general format for this is \u003ccode\u003e--format-sort field1,field2...\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe available fields are:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehasvid\u003c/code\u003e: Gives priority to formats that have a video stream\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehasaud\u003c/code\u003e: Gives priority to formats that have an audio stream\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eie_pref\u003c/code\u003e: The format preference\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003elang\u003c/code\u003e: The language preference as determined by the extractor (e.g. original language preferred over audio description)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003equality\u003c/code\u003e: The quality of the format\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003esource\u003c/code\u003e: The preference of the source\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eproto\u003c/code\u003e: Protocol used for download (\u003ccode\u003ehttps\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eftps\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ehttp\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eftp\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003em3u8_native\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003em3u8\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ehttp_dash_segments\u003c/code\u003e\u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ewebsocket_frag\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emms\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003ertsp\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ef4f\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003ef4m\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evcodec\u003c/code\u003e: Video Codec (\u003ccode\u003eav01\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp9.2\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp9\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eh265\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eh264\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp8\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eh263\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003etheora\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; other)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eacodec\u003c/code\u003e: Audio Codec (\u003ccode\u003eflac\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003ealac\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ewav\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eaiff\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eopus\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evorbis\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emp4a\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eac4\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eeac3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eac3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003edts\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; other)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecodec\u003c/code\u003e: Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003evcodec,acodec\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evext\u003c/code\u003e: Video Extension (\u003ccode\u003emp4\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emov\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eflv\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; other). If \u003ccode\u003e--prefer-free-formats\u003c/code\u003e is used, \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e is preferred.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eaext\u003c/code\u003e: Audio Extension (\u003ccode\u003em4a\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eogg\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eopus\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; other). If \u003ccode\u003e--prefer-free-formats\u003c/code\u003e is used, the order changes to \u003ccode\u003eogg\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eopus\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003ewebm\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003em4a\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eext\u003c/code\u003e: Equivalent to \u003ccode\u003evext,aext\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efilesize\u003c/code\u003e: Exact filesize, if known in advance\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efs_approx\u003c/code\u003e: Approximate filesize\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003esize\u003c/code\u003e: Exact filesize if available, otherwise approximate filesize\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eheight\u003c/code\u003e: Height of video\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewidth\u003c/code\u003e: Width of video\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eres\u003c/code\u003e: Video resolution, calculated as the smallest dimension.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efps\u003c/code\u003e: Framerate of video\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ehdr\u003c/code\u003e: The dynamic range of the video (\u003ccode\u003eDV\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eHDR12\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eHDR10+\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eHDR10\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eHLG\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eSDR\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003echannels\u003c/code\u003e: The number of audio channels\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003etbr\u003c/code\u003e: Total average bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evbr\u003c/code\u003e: Average video bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eabr\u003c/code\u003e: Average audio bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebr\u003c/code\u003e: Average bitrate in \u003ca href=\"##\" title=\"1000 bits/sec\"\u003ekbps\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etbr\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003evbr\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eabr\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003easr\u003c/code\u003e: Audio sample rate in Hz\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDeprecation warning\u003c/strong\u003e: Many of these fields have (currently undocumented) aliases, that may be removed in a future version. It is recommended to use only the documented field names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAll fields, unless specified otherwise, are sorted in descending order. To reverse this, prefix the field with a \u003ccode\u003e+\u003c/code\u003e. E.g. \u003ccode\u003e+res\u003c/code\u003e prefers format with the smallest resolution. Additionally, you can suffix a preferred value for the fields, separated by a \u003ccode\u003e:\u003c/code\u003e. E.g. \u003ccode\u003eres:720\u003c/code\u003e prefers larger videos, but no larger than 720p and the smallest video if there are no videos less than 720p. For \u003ccode\u003ecodec\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eext\u003c/code\u003e, you can provide two preferred values, the first for video and the second for audio. E.g. \u003ccode\u003e+codec:avc:m4a\u003c/code\u003e (equivalent to \u003ccode\u003e+vcodec:avc,+acodec:m4a\u003c/code\u003e) sets the video codec preference to \u003ccode\u003eh264\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eh265\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp9\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp9.2\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eav01\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evp8\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eh263\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003etheora\u003c/code\u003e and audio codec preference to \u003ccode\u003emp4a\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eaac\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003evorbis\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eopus\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003emp3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eac3\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003edts\u003c/code\u003e. You can also make the sorting prefer the nearest values to the provided by using \u003ccode\u003e~\u003c/code\u003e as the delimiter. E.g. \u003ccode\u003efilesize~1G\u003c/code\u003e prefers the format with filesize closest to 1 GiB.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe fields \u003ccode\u003ehasvid\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eie_pref\u003c/code\u003e are always given highest priority in sorting, irrespective of the user-defined order. This behavior can be changed by using \u003ccode\u003e--format-sort-force\u003c/code\u003e. Apart from these, the default order used is: \u003ccode\u003elang,quality,res,fps,hdr:12,vcodec,channels,acodec,size,br,asr,proto,ext,hasaud,source,id\u003c/code\u003e. The extractors may override this default order, but they cannot override the user-provided order.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote that the default for hdr is \u003ccode\u003ehdr:12\u003c/code\u003e; i.e. Dolby Vision is not preferred. This choice was made since DV formats are not yet fully compatible with most devices. This may be changed in the future.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf your format selector is \u003ccode\u003eworst\u003c/code\u003e, the last item is selected after sorting. This means it will select the format that is worst in all respects. Most of the time, what you actually want is the video with the smallest filesize instead. So it is generally better to use \u003ccode\u003e-f best -S +size,+br,+res,+fps\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTip\u003c/strong\u003e: You can use the \u003ccode\u003e-v -F\u003c/code\u003e to see how the formats have been sorted (worst to best).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eFormat Selection examples\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-format-selection-examples\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Format Selection examples\" href=\"#format-selection-examples\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Download and merge the best video-only format and the best audio-only format,\n# or download the best combined format if video-only format is not available\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv+ba/b\u0026quot;\n\n# Download best format that contains video,\n# and if it doesn't already have an audio stream, merge it with best audio-only format\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv*+ba/b\u0026quot;\n\n# Same as above\n$ yt-dlp\n\n# Download the best video-only format and the best audio-only format without merging them\n# For this case, an output template should be used since\n# by default, bestvideo and bestaudio will have the same file name.\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv,ba\u0026quot; -o \u0026quot;%(title)s.f%(format_id)s.%(ext)s\u0026quot;\n\n# Download and merge the best format that has a video stream,\n# and all audio-only formats into one file\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv*+mergeall[vcodec=none]\u0026quot; --audio-multistreams\n\n# Download and merge the best format that has a video stream,\n# and the best 2 audio-only formats into one file\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv*+ba+ba.2\u0026quot; --audio-multistreams\n\n\n# The following examples show the old method (without -S) of format selection\n# and how to use -S to achieve a similar but (generally) better result\n\n# Download the worst video available (old method)\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;wv*+wa/w\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video available but with the smallest resolution\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;+res\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the smallest video available\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;+size,+br\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download the best mp4 video available, or the best video if no mp4 available\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv*[ext=mp4]+ba[ext=m4a]/b[ext=mp4] / bv*+ba/b\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video with the best extension\n# (For video, mp4 \u0026gt; mov \u0026gt; webm \u0026gt; flv. For audio, m4a \u0026gt; aac \u0026gt; mp3 ...)\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;ext\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download the best video available but no better than 480p,\n# or the worst video if there is no video under 480p\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;bv*[height\u0026lt;=480]+ba/b[height\u0026lt;=480] / wv*+ba/w\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video available with the largest height but no better than 480p,\n# or the best video with the smallest resolution if there is no video under 480p\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;height:480\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video available with the largest resolution but no better than 480p,\n# or the best video with the smallest resolution if there is no video under 480p\n# Resolution is determined by using the smallest dimension.\n# So this works correctly for vertical videos as well\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;res:480\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download the best video (that also has audio) but no bigger than 50 MB,\n# or the worst video (that also has audio) if there is no video under 50 MB\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;b[filesize\u0026lt;50M] / w\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the largest video (that also has audio) but no bigger than 50 MB,\n# or the smallest video (that also has audio) if there is no video under 50 MB\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;b\u0026quot; -S \u0026quot;filesize:50M\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video (that also has audio) that is closest in size to 50 MB\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;b\u0026quot; -S \u0026quot;filesize~50M\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download best video available via direct link over HTTP/HTTPS protocol,\n# or the best video available via any protocol if there is no such video\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;(bv*+ba/b)[protocol^=http][protocol!*=dash] / (bv*+ba/b)\u0026quot;\n\n# Download best video available via the best protocol\n# (https/ftps \u0026gt; http/ftp \u0026gt; m3u8_native \u0026gt; m3u8 \u0026gt; http_dash_segments ...)\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;proto\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download the best video with either h264 or h265 codec,\n# or the best video if there is no such video\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;(bv*[vcodec~='^((he|a)vc|h26[45])']+ba) / (bv*+ba/b)\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video with best codec no better than h264,\n# or the best video with worst codec if there is no such video\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;codec:h264\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the best video with worst codec no worse than h264,\n# or the best video with best codec if there is no such video\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;+codec:h264\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# More complex examples\n\n# Download the best video no better than 720p preferring framerate greater than 30,\n# or the worst video (still preferring framerate greater than 30) if there is no such video\n$ yt-dlp -f \u0026quot;((bv*[fps\u0026gt;30]/bv*)[height\u0026lt;=720]/(wv*[fps\u0026gt;30]/wv*)) + ba / (b[fps\u0026gt;30]/b)[height\u0026lt;=720]/(w[fps\u0026gt;30]/w)\u0026quot;\n\n# Download the video with the largest resolution no better than 720p,\n# or the video with the smallest resolution available if there is no such video,\n# preferring larger framerate for formats with the same resolution\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;res:720,fps\u0026quot;\n\n\n\n# Download the video with smallest resolution no worse than 480p,\n# or the video with the largest resolution available if there is no such video,\n# preferring better codec and then larger total bitrate for the same resolution\n$ yt-dlp -S \u0026quot;+res:480,codec,br\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Download and merge the best video-only format codec no better than h264,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e or the best video with worst codec if there is no such video\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -S \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003ecodec:h264\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Download the best video with worst codec no worse than h264,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e or the best video with best codec if there is no such video\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -S \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e+codec:h264\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e More complex examples\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Download the best video no better than 720p preferring framerate greater than 30,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e or the worst video (still preferring framerate greater than 30) if there is no such video\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -f \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e((bv*[fps\u0026gt;30]/bv*)[height\u0026lt;=720]/(wv*[fps\u0026gt;30]/wv*)) + ba / (b[fps\u0026gt;30]/b)[height\u0026lt;=720]/(w[fps\u0026gt;30]/w)\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Download the video with the largest resolution no better than 720p,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e or the video with the smallest resolution available if there is no such video,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e preferring larger framerate for formats with the same resolution\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -S \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eres:720,fps\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Download the video with smallest resolution no worse than 480p,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e or the video with the largest resolution available if there is no such video,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e preferring better codec and then larger total bitrate for the same resolution\u003c/span\u003e\n$ yt-dlp -S \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e+res:480,codec,br\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch1 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMODIFYING METADATA\u003c/h1\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-modifying-metadata\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: MODIFYING METADATA\" href=\"#modifying-metadata\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe metadata obtained by the extractors can be modified by using \u003ccode\u003e--parse-metadata\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e--replace-in-metadata\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e--replace-in-metadata FIELDS REGEX REPLACE\u003c/code\u003e is used to replace text in any metadata field using \u003ca href=\"https://docs.python.org/3/library/re.html#regular-expression-syntax\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ePython regular expression\u003c/a\u003e. \u003ca href=\"https://docs.python.org/3/library/re.html?highlight=backreferences#re.sub\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eBackreferences\u003c/a\u003e can be used in the replace string for advanced use.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe general syntax of \u003ccode\u003e--parse-metadata FROM:TO\u003c/code\u003e is to give the name of a field or an \u003ca href=\"#output-template\"\u003eoutput template\u003c/a\u003e to extract data from, and the format to interpret it as, separated by a colon \u003ccode\u003e:\u003c/code\u003e. Either a \u003ca href=\"https://docs.python.org/3/library/re.html#regular-expression-syntax\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003ePython regular expression\u003c/a\u003e with named capture groups, a single field name, or a similar syntax to the \u003ca href=\"#output-template\"\u003eoutput template\u003c/a\u003e (only \u003ccode\u003e%(field)s\u003c/code\u003e formatting is supported) can be used for \u003ccode\u003eTO\u003c/code\u003e. The option can be used multiple times to parse and modify various fields.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote that these options preserve their relative order, allowing replacements to be made in parsed fields and vice versa. Also, any field thus created can be used in the \u003ca href=\"#output-template\"\u003eoutput template\u003c/a\u003e and will also affect the media file's metadata added when using \u003ccode\u003e--embed-metadata\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis option also has a few special uses:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can download an additional URL based on the metadata of the currently downloaded video. To do this, set the field \u003ccode\u003eadditional_urls\u003c/code\u003e to the URL that you want to download. E.g. \u003ccode\u003e--parse-metadata \"description:(?P\u0026lt;additional_urls\u0026gt;https?://www\\.vimeo\\.com/\\d+)\"\u003c/code\u003e will download the first vimeo video found in the description\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can use this to change the metadata that is embedded in the media file. To do this, set the value of the corresponding field with a \u003ccode\u003emeta_\u003c/code\u003e prefix. For example, any value you set to \u003ccode\u003emeta_description\u003c/code\u003e field will be added to the \u003ccode\u003edescription\u003c/code\u003e field in the file - you can use this to set a different \"description\" and \"synopsis\". To modify the metadata of individual streams, use the \u003ccode\u003emeta\u0026lt;n\u0026gt;_\u003c/code\u003e prefix (e.g. \u003ccode\u003emeta1_language\u003c/code\u003e). Any value set to the \u003ccode\u003emeta_\u003c/code\u003e field will overwrite all default values.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote\u003c/strong\u003e: Metadata modification happens before format selection, post-extraction and other post-processing operations. Some fields may be added or changed during these steps, overriding your changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor reference, these are the fields yt-dlp adds by default to the file data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Interpret the title as \u0026quot;Artist - Title\u0026quot;\n$ yt-dlp --parse-metadata \u0026quot;title:%(artist)s - %(title)s\u0026quot;\n\n# Regex example\n$ \u0026quot;%(series)s S%(season_number)02dE%(episode_number)02d:%(title)s\u0026quot;\n\n# Prioritize uploader as the \u0026quot;artist\u0026quot; field in video metadata\n$ yt-dlp --parse-metadata metadata\n$ yt-dlp --parse-metadata \u0026quot;:(?P\u0026lt;meta_synopsis\u0026gt;)\u0026quot;\n\n# Remove \u0026quot;formats\u0026quot; field from the infojson by setting it to an empty string\n$ \u003ccode\u003e--extractor-args KEY:ARGS\u003c/code\u003e. \u003ccode\u003eARGS\u003c/code\u003e is a \u003ccode\u003e;\u003c/code\u003e (semicolon) separated string of \u003ccode\u003eARG=VAL1,VAL2\u003c/code\u003e. E.g. \u003ccode\u003e--extractor-args \"youtube:player-client=tv,mweb;formats=incomplete\" --extractor-args \"twitter:api=syndication\"\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote: In CLI, \u003ccode\u003eARG\u003c/code\u003e can use \u003ccode\u003e-\u003c/code\u003e instead of \u003ccode\u003e_\u003c/code\u003e; e.g. \u003ccode\u003eyoutube:player-client\"\u003c/code\u003e becomes \u003ccode\u003eyoutube:player_client\"\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe following extractors use this feature:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eyoutube\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-youtube\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: youtube\" href=\"#youtube\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003elang\u003c/code\u003e: Prefer translated metadata (\u003ccode\u003etitle\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003edescription\u003c/code\u003e etc) of this language code (case-sensitive). By default, the video primary language metadata is preferred, with a fallback to \u003ccode\u003een\u003c/code\u003e translated. See \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/blob/415b4c9f955b1a0391204bd24a7132590e7b3bdb/yt_dlp/extractor/youtube/_base.py#L402-L409\"\u003eyoutube/_base.py\u003c/a\u003e for the list of supported content language codes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eskip\u003c/code\u003e: One or more of \u003ccode\u003ehls\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003edash\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003etranslated_subs\u003c/code\u003e to skip extraction of the m3u8 manifests, dash manifests and \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/4090#issuecomment-1158102032\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/4090/hovercard\"\u003eauto-translated subtitles\u003c/a\u003e respectively\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplayer_client\u003c/code\u003e: Clients to extract video data from. The currently available clients are \u003ccode\u003eweb\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_safari\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_embedded\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_music\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_creator\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emweb\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eios\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eandroid\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eandroid_sdkless\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eandroid_vr\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etv\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etv_simply\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etv_downgraded\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003etv_embedded\u003c/code\u003e. By default, \u003ccode\u003etv,android_sdkless,web\u003c/code\u003e is used. If no JavaScript runtime/engine is available, then \u003ccode\u003eandroid_sdkless,web_safari,web\u003c/code\u003e is used. If logged-in cookies are passed to yt-dlp, then \u003ccode\u003etv_downgraded,web_safari,web\u003c/code\u003e is used for free accounts and \u003ccode\u003etv_downgraded,web_creator,web\u003c/code\u003e is used for premium accounts. The \u003ccode\u003eweb_music\u003c/code\u003e client is added for \u003ccode\u003emusic.youtube.com\u003c/code\u003e URLs when logged-in cookies are used. The \u003ccode\u003eweb_embedded\u003c/code\u003e client is added for age-restricted videos but only works if the video is embeddable. The \u003ccode\u003etv_embedded\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eweb_creator\u003c/code\u003e clients are added for age-restricted videos if account age-verification is required. Some clients, such as \u003ccode\u003eweb\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eweb_music\u003c/code\u003e, require a \u003ccode\u003epo_token\u003c/code\u003e for their formats to be downloadable. Some clients, such as \u003ccode\u003eweb_creator\u003c/code\u003e, will only work with authentication. Not all clients support authentication via cookies. You can use \u003ccode\u003edefault\u003c/code\u003e for the default clients, or you can use \u003ccode\u003eall\u003c/code\u003e for all clients (not recommended). You can prefix a client with \u003ccode\u003e-\u003c/code\u003e to exclude it, e.g. \u003ccode\u003eyoutube:player_client=default,-ios\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplayer_skip\u003c/code\u003e: Skip some network requests that are generally needed for robust extraction. One or more of \u003ccode\u003econfigs\u003c/code\u003e (skip client configs), \u003ccode\u003ewebpage\u003c/code\u003e (skip initial webpage), \u003ccode\u003ejs\u003c/code\u003e (skip js player), \u003ccode\u003einitial_data\u003c/code\u003e (skip initial data/next ep request). While these options can help reduce the number of requests needed or avoid some rate-limiting, they could cause issues such as missing formats or metadata.  See \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/pull/860\" data-hovercard-type=\"pull_request\" data-hovercard-url=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/pull/860/hovercard\"\u003e#860\u003c/a\u003e and \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/12826\" data-hovercard-type=\"issue\" data-hovercard-url=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/issues/12826/hovercard\"\u003e#12826\u003c/a\u003e for more details\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ewebpage_skip\u003c/code\u003e: Skip extraction of embedded webpage data. One or both of \u003ccode\u003eplayer_response\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003einitial_data\u003c/code\u003e. These options are for testing purposes and don't skip any network requests\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplayer_params\u003c/code\u003e: YouTube player parameters to use for player requests. Will overwrite any default ones set by yt-dlp.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplayer_js_variant\u003c/code\u003e: The player javascript variant to use for n/sig deciphering. The known variants are: \u003ccode\u003emain\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etcc\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etce\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ees5\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ees6\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etv\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etv_es6\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ephone\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etablet\u003c/code\u003e. The default is \u003ccode\u003emain\u003c/code\u003e, and the others are for debugging purposes. You can use \u003ccode\u003eactual\u003c/code\u003e to go with what is prescribed by the site\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eplayer_js_version\u003c/code\u003e: The player javascript version to use for n/sig deciphering, in the format of \u003ccode\u003esignature_timestamp@hash\u003c/code\u003e (e.g. \u003ccode\u003e20348@0004de42\u003c/code\u003e). The default is to use what is prescribed by the site, and can be selected with \u003ccode\u003eactual\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecomment_sort\u003c/code\u003e: \u003ccode\u003etop\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003enew\u003c/code\u003e (default) - choose comment sorting mode (on YouTube's side)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emax_comments\u003c/code\u003e: Limit the amount of comments to gather. Comma-separated list of integers representing \u003ccode\u003emax-comments,max-parents,max-replies,max-replies-per-thread\u003c/code\u003e. Default is \u003ccode\u003eall,all,all,all\u003c/code\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eE.g. \u003ccode\u003eall,all,1000,10\u003c/code\u003e will get a maximum of 1000 replies total, with up to 10 replies per thread. \u003ccode\u003e1000,all,100\u003c/code\u003e will get a maximum of 1000 comments, with a maximum of 100 replies total\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eformats\u003c/code\u003e: Change the types of formats to return. \u003ccode\u003edashy\u003c/code\u003e (convert HTTP to DASH), \u003ccode\u003eduplicate\u003c/code\u003e (identical content but different URLs or protocol; includes \u003ccode\u003edashy\u003c/code\u003e), \u003ccode\u003eincomplete\u003c/code\u003e (cannot be downloaded completely - live dash and post-live m3u8), \u003ccode\u003emissing_pot\u003c/code\u003e (include formats that require a PO Token but are missing one)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003einnertube_host\u003c/code\u003e: Innertube API host to use for all API requests; e.g. \u003ccode\u003estudio.youtube.com\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eyoutubei.googleapis.com\u003c/code\u003e. Note that cookies exported from one subdomain will not work on others\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003einnertube_key\u003c/code\u003e: Innertube API key to use for all API requests. By default, no API key is used\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eraise_incomplete_data\u003c/code\u003e: \u003ccode\u003eIncomplete Data Received\u003c/code\u003e raises an error instead of reporting a warning\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edata_sync_id\u003c/code\u003e: Overrides the account Data Sync ID used in Innertube API requests. This may be needed if you are using an account with \u003ccode\u003eyoutube:player_skip=webpage,configs\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eyoutubetab:skip=webpage\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evisitor_data\u003c/code\u003e: Overrides the Visitor Data used in Innertube API requests. This should be used with \u003ccode\u003eplayer_skip=webpage,configs\u003c/code\u003e and without cookies. Note: this may have adverse effects if used improperly. If a session from a browser is wanted, you should pass cookies instead (which contain the Visitor ID)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003epo_token\u003c/code\u003e:  Proof of Origin (PO) Token(s) to use. Comma-separated list of PO Tokens in the format \u003ccode\u003eCLIENT.CONTEXT+PO_TOKEN\u003c/code\u003e, e.g. \u003ccode\u003eyoutube:po_token=web.gvs+XXX,web.player=XXX,web_safari.gvs+YYY\u003c/code\u003e. Context can be any of \u003ccode\u003egvs\u003c/code\u003e (Google Video Server URLs), \u003ccode\u003eplayer\u003c/code\u003e (Innertube player request) or \u003ccode\u003esubs\u003c/code\u003e (Subtitles)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003epot_trace\u003c/code\u003e: Enable debug logging for PO Token fetching. Either \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e (default)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003efetch_pot\u003c/code\u003e: Policy to use for fetching a PO Token from providers. One of \u003ccode\u003ealways\u003c/code\u003e (always try fetch a PO Token regardless if the client requires one for the given context), \u003ccode\u003enever\u003c/code\u003e (never fetch a PO Token), or \u003ccode\u003eauto\u003c/code\u003e (default; only fetch a PO Token if the client requires one for the given context)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ejsc_trace\u003c/code\u003e: Enable debug logging for JS Challenge fetching. Either \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e (default)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003euse_ad_playback_context\u003c/code\u003e: Skip preroll ads to eliminate the mandatory wait period before download. Do NOT use this when passing premium account cookies to yt-dlp, as it will result in a loss of premium formats. Only effective with the \u003ccode\u003eweb\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_safari\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eweb_music\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003emweb\u003c/code\u003e player clients. This respects underscore prefix (e.g. \u003ccode\u003e_MyBasePluginIE\u003c/code\u003e is private) and \u003ccode\u003e__all__\u003c/code\u003e. Since the extractor replaces the parent, you should exclude the subclass extractor from being imported separately by making it private using one of the methods described above.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf you are a plugin author, add \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/topics/yt-dlp-plugins\"\u003eyt-dlp-plugins\u003c/a\u003e as a topic to your repository for discoverability.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSee the \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md#developer-instructions\"\u003eDeveloper Instructions\u003c/a\u003e on how to write and test an extractor.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch1 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eEMBEDDING YT-DLP\u003c/h1\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-embedding-yt-dlp\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: EMBEDDING YT-DLP\" href=\"#embedding-yt-dlp\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eyt-dlp makes the best effort to be a good command-line program, and thus should be callable from any programming language.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYour program should avoid parsing the normal stdout since they may change in future versions. Instead, they should use options such as \u003ccode\u003e-J\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--print\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--progress-template\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--exec\u003c/code\u003e etc to create console output that you can reliably reproduce and parse.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFrom a Python program, you can embed yt-dlp in a more powerful fashion, like this:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from yt_dlp import YoutubeDL\n\nURLS = ['https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BaW_jenozKc']\nwith YoutubeDL() as ydl:\n    ydl.download(URLS)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eyt_dlp\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eYoutubeDL\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eURLS\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e [\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BaW_jenozKc'\u003c/span\u003e]\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ewith\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eYoutubeDL\u003c/span\u003e() \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eas\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eydl\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eydl\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003edownload\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eURLS\u003c/span\u003e)\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eMost likely, you'll want to use various options. and the best audio that won't result in an mkv.\n    NOTE: This is just an example and does not handle all cases \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n\n    # formats are already sorted worst to best\n    formats = ctx.get('formats')[::-1]\n\n    # acodec='none' means there is no audio\n    best_video = next(f for f in formats\n                      if f['vcodec'] != 'none' and f['acodec'] == 'none')\n\n    # find compatible audio extension\n    audio_ext = {'mp4': 'm4a', 'webm': 'webm'}[best_video['ext']]\n    # vcodec='none' means there is no video\n    best_audio = next(f for f in format_selector,\n}\n\nwith yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:\n    ydl.download(URLS)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan Use \u003ccode\u003e--concurrent-fragments\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e-N\u003c/code\u003e) option to set the number of threads used\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAria2c with HLS/DASH\u003c/strong\u003e: You can use \u003ccode\u003earia2c\u003c/code\u003e as the external downloader for DASH(mpd) and HLS(m3u8) formats\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNew and fixed extractors\u003c/strong\u003e: Many new extractors have been added and a lot of existing ones have been fixed. See the \u003ca href=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/blob/master/Changelog.md\"\u003echangelog\u003c/a\u003e or the \u003ca href=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/blob/master/supportedsites.md\"\u003elist of supported sites\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNew MSOs\u003c/strong\u003e: Philo, Spectrum, SlingTV, Cablevision, RCN etc.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSubtitle extraction from manifests\u003c/strong\u003e: Subtitles can be extracted from streaming media manifests. See \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/commit/be6202f12b97858b9d716e608394b51065d0419f\"\u003ecommit/be6202f\u003c/a\u003e for details\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMultiple paths and output templates\u003c/strong\u003e: You can give different \u003ca href=\"#output-template\"\u003eoutput templates\u003c/a\u003e and download paths for different types of files. You can also set a temporary path where intermediary files are downloaded to using \u003ccode\u003e--paths\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003e-P\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePortable Configuration\u003c/strong\u003e: Configuration files are automatically loaded from the home and root directories. See \u003ca href=\"#configuration\"\u003eCONFIGURATION\u003c/a\u003e for details\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOutput template improvements\u003c/strong\u003e: Output templates can now have date-time formatting, numeric offsets, object traversal etc. See \u003ca href=\"#output-template\"\u003eoutput template\u003c/a\u003e for details. Even more advanced operations can also be done with the help of \u003ccode\u003e--parse-metadata\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e--replace-in-metadata\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOther new options\u003c/strong\u003e: Many new options have been added such as \u003ccode\u003e--alias\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--print\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--concat-playlist\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--wait-for-video\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--retry-sleep\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--sleep-requests\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--convert-thumbnails\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--force-download-archive\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--force-overwrites\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--break-match-filters\u003c/code\u003e etc\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImprovements\u003c/strong\u003e: Regex and other operators in \u003ccode\u003e--format\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003e--match-filters\u003c/code\u003e, multiple \u003ccode\u003e--postprocessor-args\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e--downloader-args\u003c/code\u003e, faster archive checking, more \u003ca href=\"#format-selection\"\u003eformat selection options\u003c/a\u003e, merge multi-video/audio, multiple \u003ccode\u003e--config-locations\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e--exec\u003c/code\u003e at different stages, etc\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePlugins\u003c/strong\u003e: Extractors and PostProcessors can be loaded from an external file. See \u003ca href=\"#plugins\"\u003eplugins\u003c/a\u003e for details\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSelf updater\u003c/strong\u003e: The releases can be updated using \u003ccode\u003eyt-dlp -U\u003c/code\u003e, and downgraded using \u003ccode\u003e--update-to\u003c/code\u003e if required\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAutomated builds\u003c/strong\u003e: \u003ca href=\"#update-channels\"\u003eNightly/master builds\u003c/a\u003e can be used with \u003ccode\u003e--update-to nightly\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e--update-to master\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSee \u003ca href=\"/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/blob/master/Changelog.md\"\u003echangelog\u003c/a\u003e or \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/yt-dlp/yt-dlp/commits\"\u003ecommits\u003c/a\u003e for the full list of changes\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFeatures marked with a \u003cstrong\u003e*\u003c/strong\u003e have been back-ported to youtube-dl\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\"
